<script type="text/javascript">

    function DepartmentChange() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        DepartmentChange(grid);
    }

    $("#btnMassUpdateEmployee__EmployeesDataView").click(function () {

        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("EmployeesDataView");

        if (!$("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation."))
            return;

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowMassUpdateEmployee")
                         .SetContent({ type: "POST", url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassUpdateEmployee" })
                         .SetIsModal(true)
                         .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                         .SetonActivate(function () { RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeMassUpdate", null); })
                         .SetHeight('70%')
                         .SetWidth(900)
                         .SetTitle('Mass Update Employee')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    function EditEmployee(EmployeeId) {

        var id = EmployeeId;
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        EditEmployeeFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    function EditEmployeeFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        data = { Id: id, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DetailsPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowGoToSource")
               .SetTitle('Edit Employee')
               .SetContent(options)
               .SetWidth('1220')
               .SetHeight('90%')
               .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    }
    function OnPageLoad() {

        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "EmployeesDataView");
        //todo: move to page of grid that was last viewed.
        //RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#EmployeesDataView");

        $("#btnAdd__EmployeesDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            options = { url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CreatePopup", data: {sourceDataView: 'EmployeesDataView' }, type: "POST" };
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowGoToSource")
           .SetTitle('Add Employee')
           .SetContent(options)
           .SetWidth('1220')
           .SetHeight('90%')
           .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)

            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

        });

        $("#btnEdit__EmployeesDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var grid = $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView");
            if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
                var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                EditEmployeeFinsWindow(0, aptaDataViewSelection);

            }

        });

        function DeleteEmployees() {

            var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            //debugger;
            var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("EmployeesDataView");

            $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
                url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MultipleDelete?" + "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds,
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (returnData) {
                    NavigateTo("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/Search");
                }
            });
        };

        $("#btnDelete__EmployeesDataView").click(function (e) {

            var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("EmployeesDataView");

            if (ValidateGridSelection("EmployeesDataView", true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation."))
                ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected employees", DeleteEmployees);

        });

        function MassApproveJobs() {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/QAAutom/Employee/IsActiveJobInMassApproveSelectedEmployees",
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (returnData) {
                    //debugger;
                    if (!returnData) {
                        //redirect to Mass Job approve grid
                        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassApproveJob";
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowYesNoDialog("Mass Approve", "One or more of the selected jobs may be part of a Payroll Register that is currently being processed. Any changes that have been made to the job(s) will not affect this register. To have the changes apply to the in-process register, the job(s) will have to be removed from the register before running this process. Do you want to continue with the Mass Job Approval?", function () {
                            window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassApproveJob";
                        });
                    }

                },
                error: function (e) {
                    //debugger;
                }
            });

        }

        function ReturnFromSalaryFormulaPopup() {

        }

        function MassUpdateSalaries() {

            var kendoWindow = $("#popupwindowMassUpdateSalaries").kendoWindow({
                content: { url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/SalarySpecification" },
                title: "Specify Salary Update Formula",
                modal: true,
                deactivate: ReturnFromSalaryFormulaPopup,
                refresh: function (e) { e.sender.center(); }
            });

            kendoWindow.data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        }

        function MassIncrementSalarySchedule() {

            window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassIncrementSalarySchedule";

        }

        function returnFromIncrementEmployeeExperience() {

        }
        function OpenIncrementEmployeeExperienceWnd() {

            var finsWindow =
                FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowIncrementEmployeeExperience")
                    .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IncrementExperience" })
                    .SetIsModal(true)
                    .SetonClose(returnFromIncrementEmployeeExperience)
                    .SetTitle("Increment Employee Experience")
                    .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                    .SetWidth(500)
                    .SetHeight(150)
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeIncrementExperience", null);
        }

        $('#btnMassApproveJob__EmployeesDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            MassApproveJobs();
        });

        $('#btnMassUpdateSalaries__EmployeesDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            MassUpdateSalaries();
        });

        $('#btnIncrementEmployeeExperience__EmployeesDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            OpenIncrementEmployeeExperienceWnd();
        });

        $('#btnMassIncrementSalarySchedule__EmployeesDataView').click(function () {
            MassIncrementSalarySchedule();
        });

        $('#btnEnableEmployee__EmployeesDataView').click(function () {
            ConfirmSetEnabledEmployee("True");
        });

        $('#btnDisableEmployee__EmployeesDataView').click(function () {
            ConfirmSetEnabledEmployee("False");
        });

        $('#btnRolloverEmployeeJobs__EmployeesDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            OpenRolloverEmployeeJobWnd();
        });

        $('#btnCalculateEvaluations__EmployeesDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            ConfirmCalcEmpEvaluations();
        });

    }

    function ConfirmCalcEmpEvaluations() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
        }
        else {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Calculate Composite Score", "Are you sure you want to calculate evaluations for selected employee(s)?", CalculateEmployeeEvaluations);
        }
    }

    function RefreshOnCalculateEmployeeEvaluations(selectedRowIds) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        var key = "EmployeeSearch";
        $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/EvaluationsCalculate',
                     { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, isMultiEmployees: true, operationResultId: massOperationId, key: key },
                '', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function CalculateEmployeeEvaluations() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnCalculateEmployeeEvaluations(selectedRowIds); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    $(document).ready(function () { OnPageLoad(); });

    function ReturnFromRolloverEmployeeJobWnd() {

    }
    function OpenRolloverEmployeeJobWnd() {

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IsNextCycleAvailable',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if (!result) {
                    ShowOkDialog("Notice", "No next cycle available for rollover job process.", null);
                    return;
                }

                var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowRolloverEmployeeJob")
                                        .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/RolloverEmployeeJob" }).SetIsModal(true).SetHeight(430).SetWidth(640)
                .SetTitle('Rollover Employee Jobs').SetonDeactivate(function () { UnRegisterActiveScreen(); });
                finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            }
        });

    }

    function ConfirmSetEnabledEmployee(enabled) {
        if (enabled == "True") {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Enable Employee(s)", "Are you sure that you want to enable selected employee(s)? Only disabled employee(s) will be enabled.", EnableEmployees);
        }
        else {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Disable Employee(s)", "Are you sure that you want to disable selected employee(s)? Only enabled employee(s) will be disabled.", DisableEmployees);
        }
    }
    function EnableEmployees()
    { SetEnabledEmployees("True"); }
    function DisableEmployees()
    { SetEnabledEmployees("False"); }
    function SetEnabledEmployees(enabled) {
        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/SetEnabledEmployees?" + "enabled=" + enabled + "&amp;selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (returnData) {
                NavigateTo("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/Search");

            }
        });
    }

    $("#btnAdd__EmployeesScreen").click(function (e) {
        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/Create";

    });

    $("#btnEdit__EmployeesScreen").click(function (e) {
        if (!$("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MultipleEdit",
            dataType: "json",
        success: function (returnData) {
            if (returnData) {
                window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/Details/" + returnData.EmployeeId;
            }

        }
    });

    });

                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }

    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }

    var loadTabJob = true;
    var loadTabAddress = true;
    var loadTabContact = true;

    function ReturnFromLeave() {

        var leaveTypeId = $('#LeaveTypeId').val();
        var data = { LeaveTypeId: leaveTypeId, EmployeeId: '622' };

        $("#divEmployeeLeavesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/GetLeaveData",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (data) {
                var grid = $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                if (data.optionalParameters) {
                    $("#divEmployeeLeavesDataView").data("AptaDataView").SetDataParameters(data.optionalParameters)
                }
                grid.dataSource.one("requestEnd", function () { GridLeaveRequestEnd(data.LeaveTaken, data.LeaveAvailable); });
                grid.dataSource.query({ page: 1, pageSize: grid.dataSource.pageSize(), sort: grid.dataSource.sort(), group: grid.dataSource.group() });
            },
            error: function (e) {
                //
            }
        });
    }
    function ReturnFromAddress() {
        $("#divEmployeeAddressesDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();
    }

    function ReturnFromContact() {
        $("#divEmployeeContactsDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();

    {

    }

    function onActivate(e) {
        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        var activeTabStripText = $("#EMPTabStrip").data("FINSUITabStrip").GetActiveTabText()
        if (activeTabStripText == "Addresses") {
            if (loadTabAddress) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeAddressesDataView();
                var gridAdd = $("#EmployeeAddressesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabAddress = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeAddressesDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == 'Deduction Sets') {
            if (loadDedcutionAsssignments) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView();
                loadDedcutionAsssignments = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Jobs") {

            if (loadTabJob) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView();
                var gridAdd = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabJob = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeJobsDataView");
        }

        else if (activeTabStripText == "Contacts") {
            if (loadTabContact) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeContactsDataView();
                var gridContact = $("#EmployeeContactsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabContact = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeContactsDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Certificates") {
            if (loadTabCertificate) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeCertificatesDataView();
                var gridCertificate = $("#EmployeeCertificatesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabCertificate = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeCertificatesDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Extended Leave") {
            if (loadExtendedLeave) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeExtendedLeavesDataView();
                var grid = $("#EmployeeExtendedLeavesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadExtendedLeave = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeExtendedLeavesDataView");
        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Leave Detail") {
            //var gridLeaves = $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (loadTabLeaves) {
                loadTabLeaves = false;
                $('#divEmployeeLeavesDataView').hide();
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail","Employee" , "EmployeeLeavesDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Education History") {
            if (loadTabEducationHistory) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeEducationHistoryDataView();
                var grdEducationHistory = $("#EmployeeEducationHistoryDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabEducationHistory = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeEducationHistoryDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Position History") {
            if (loadPositionHistory) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeePositionHistoryDataView();
                var gridPositionHistory = $("#EmployeePositionHistoryDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadPositionHistory = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeePositionHistoryDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Attached Files") {
            var gridAttachments = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (loadEmployeeAttachments) {
                loadEmployeeAttachments = false;
                gridAttachments.dataSource.read();
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "Employee", "AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Assignments") {
            if (loadEmployeeAssignments) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeAssignmentsDataView();
                var gridAssignments = $("#EmployeeAssignmentsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadEmployeeAssignments = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeAssignmentsDataView");

        }
        else if(activeTabStripText == 'Deductions')
        {
            if (loadDeductionSetupTab) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeDeductionDetailDataView();
                loadDeductionSetupTab = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeDeductionDetailDataView");
        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Electronic Delivery") {
            if (loadEmployeeElectronicDelivery) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeElectronicDeliveryDataView();
                var gridElectronicDelivery = $("#EmployeeElectronicDeliveryDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadEmployeeElectronicDelivery = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "EmployeeElectronicDeliveryDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Appointments") {
            if (loadEmployeeAppointments) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeAppointmentsDataView();
                var gridAssignments = $("#EmployeeAppointmentsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadEmployeeAppointments = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeAppointmentsDataView");

                loadEmployeeEvaluations = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeEvaluationDataView");

        }

    }

<script>

    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("#showMaskedValue_SSNLabel").click(function () {

            var Id = $("#hdnMaskedValue_SSNLabel").val();
            var buttonText = $("#showMaskedValue_SSNLabel").text();
            var showValue = buttonText.indexOf("(Show)") &gt; -1;
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/QAAutom/AptaFundBase/ShowMaskedValue",
                data: {
                    ControlType: 'SSN', Id: Id, showValue: showValue
                },
                cache: false,
                dataType: 'json',
                error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                },
                success: function (response) {
                    if (response.Success == true) {
                        if ('SSN' != 'VendorTaxId') {
                            $("#lblSSNValue_SSNLabel").text(response.Value);
                        }
                        else {
                            $("#lblVendorTaxIdValue_SSNLabel").text(response.Value);
                        }
                        $("#showMaskedValue_SSNLabel").text(response.buttonText);
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });
</script>

<script>
    function GetLeaveGridData() {
        var leaveTypeId = $('#LeaveTypeId').val();
        var data = { LeaveTypeId: leaveTypeId, EmployeeId: '622' };

        //ajax call for grid read on basis of Leave Type Id
        $("#divEmployeeLeavesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/GetLeaveData",
            data: data,
        dataType: "json",
        success: function (data) {
            var grid = $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (data.optionalParameters) {
                $("#divEmployeeLeavesDataView").data("AptaDataView").SetDataParameters(data.optionalParameters)
            }
            grid.dataSource.one("requestEnd", function () { GridLeaveRequestEnd(data.LeaveTaken, data.LeaveAvailable); });
            grid.dataSource.query({ page: 1, pageSize: grid.dataSource.pageSize(), sort: grid.dataSource.sort(), group: grid.dataSource.group() });

            $('#divEmployeeLeavesDataView').show();
        },
        error: function (e) {
            //
        }
    });
    }
</script>

<script>

    function EmployeeLeavesDataView__Restore() {
        var leaveTypeId = $('#LeaveTypeId').val();
        var data = { LeaveTypeId: leaveTypeId, EmployeeId: '622' };
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/GetLeaveData",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (data) {
                GridLeaveRequestEnd(data.LeaveTaken, data.LeaveAvailable);
            },
            error: function (e) {
                //
            }
        });
    }

    function GridLeaveRequestEnd(LeaveTaken, AvailableLeaves) {

        //update grid header with data
        //debugger;
        var leaveType = $('#LeaveTypeId').data("kendoDropDownList").text();
        if (leaveType === "Personal") {
            $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView thead [data-field=pyEmployeeLeaveTaken__LeaveTaken] .k-link").html("Amount (Hours)");
        }
        else {
            $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView thead [data-field=pyEmployeeLeaveTaken__LeaveTaken] .k-link").html("Amount (Days)");
        }

        var Taken = 'Leave Taken: ' + LeaveTaken;
        var Available = 'Available Leave: ' + AvailableLeaves;

        setTimeout(function () { showFooterText(Taken, Available); }, 900);
    }

    function showFooterText(LeaveTaken, LeaveAvailable) {
        $('#LeaveTaken__Footer').text(LeaveTaken);
        $('#LeaveComment__Footer').text(LeaveAvailable);
    }

    function IsEmployeeInPayroll() {
                    var ddlLeaveTypeId = $("#LeaveTypeId").data("kendoDropDownList");
                            ddlLeaveTypeId.enable(false);
                            $('#btnAdd__EmployeeLeavesDataView').unbind('click');
                            $('#btnEdit__EmployeeLeavesDataView').unbind('click');
                            $('#btnDelete__EmployeeLeavesDataView').unbind('click');
                    $('#divFormEmployeeLeaveErrors').html("Leave information cannot be displayed if employee is disabled or not yet submitted to payroll.");
                            $('#divFormEmployeeLeaveErrors').addClass("global_message notice");
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {
        IsEmployeeInPayroll();
    });
</script>

<script>

	$(document).ready(function () {
        function ReturnFromAttachmentPopup__EmployeeManagement() {
            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            grid.dataSource.read();
            UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        }

        $("#btnAdd__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement").click(function () {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowAttachmentFramework__EmployeeManagement")
                      .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/AddAttachment?ScreenName=EmployeeManagement" + "&amp;ObjectKey1=622" + "&amp;ObjectKey2=-1" + "&amp;ObjectKey3=" })
                      .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(ReturnFromAttachmentPopup__EmployeeManagement)
                      .SetTitle("Add Attachment")
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "frmAttachment__EmployeeManagement", "AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement");
        });

        $("#btnEdit__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement").click(function () {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
                return;
            }

            var gridData = grid.dataSource.data();
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; gridData.length; i++) {
                if (gridData[i].Id == selectedRowIds &amp;&amp; gridData[i].syViewFileAttachments__ScreenName != 'EmployeeManagement') {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Linked attachment cannot be edited", "error");
                    return;
                }
            }

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowAttachmentFramework__EmployeeManagement")
                      .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/EditAttachment?FileId=" + selectedRowIds })
                      .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(ReturnFromAttachmentPopup__EmployeeManagement)
                      .SetTitle("Edit Attachment")
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "frmAttachment__EmployeeManagement", "AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement");
        });

        $("#btnDelete__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement").click(function () {
            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0) {
                ShowYesNoDialog('Confirm Delete', 'Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?', DeleteAttachments);
            }
            else {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            }
        });

        function DeleteAttachments() {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(MassActionResultRefresh).
    SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen);
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
        }

        function MassActionResultRefresh()
        {
            var massActionId = GetMassActionId();
            $("#divAttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/GridConfig/DeleteAttachment',
				{ massOpertaionId: massActionId, dataView: "AttachmentFrameworkDataView" },
                    '', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        //removing selection from the attributes.
                        grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected", "");
                        grid.thead.find("tr .selectAll__AttachmentFrameworkDataView").attr("checked", false);
                        SetGridSelectedRecords("AttachmentFrameworkDataView", "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        //refresh grid
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
        }

        $("#btnView__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement").click(function () {

            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
                return;
			}
			window.location.href = "/QAAutom/GridConfig/ViewAttachment" + "?dataView=AttachmentFrameworkDataView";

        });

    });
</script>

            Apply: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/ApplyNamedGridSettings'
        };

        var msgs = {

            Delete: "Record deleted successfully.",
            ConfirmDelete: "Confirm Delete",
            DeleteSelectedRecords: "Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?"
        };

        UserGridSettingsMenuReturn('/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', e, 'AttachmentFrameworkDataView', urls.GetNamedGridSettings, dataViewSettings, urls.Apply,
                                    function (e) {
                                        UserGridSettingsMenuOnSelect(e, '/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', 'AttachmentFrameworkDataView', dataViewSettings, urls, msgs)

    }

    var eventArgs;
    $("#btnSubmitEmployeeToPayroll__Employee").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        eventArgs = e;
        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm", "Are you sure you want to submit selected employee(s) to payroll?", function () {
            ShowPayrollTransactionDateDialog("True", "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployee/ShowTransactionEncumbranceDialog",
                SubmitEmployeeToPayrollFunction, "SubmitEmployeeToPayrollFunction", null , "622~5", "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployee/IsAtleastOneJobWithEncumbranceExists"
                    , "Submit Employee To Payroll", "Employee", "")
        });
    });

    function SubmitEmployeeToPayrollFunction(transactionDate)
    {
        SubmitEmployeeToPayroll(eventArgs, 622,5,0, transactionDate);
    }

    $("#btnRemoveEmployeeFromPayroll__Employee").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        eventArgs = e;
        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm", "Are you sure you want to remove selected employee(s) from payroll?", function () {
            ShowPayrollTransactionDateDialog("True", "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployee/ShowTransactionEncumbranceDialog",
                RemoveEmployeeToPayrollFunction, "RemoveEmployeeToPayrollFunction", null , "622~5", "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployee/IsAtleastOneJobWithEncumbranceExists"
                    , "Remove Employee From Payroll", "Employee", "")
        });
    });

    function RemoveEmployeeToPayrollFunction(transactionDate)
    {
        RemoveEmployeeFromPayroll(eventArgs, 622,5,0, transactionDate);
    }

    function SubmitEmployeeToPayroll(e,EmployeeId,CycleId,PayrollCycleId, transactionDate) {
        var data;
        data = { EmployeeId: EmployeeId, CycleId: CycleId, PayrollCycleId: PayrollCycleId, transactionDate: transactionDate };

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/SubmitEmployeeToPayroll",
            data: data,
            type: "POST",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {

                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DetailsPopup",data: { id : '622', sourceDataView :  'EmployeesDataView' ,aptaDataViewSelection:aptaDataViewSelection},type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","EmployeeDetail_Error");
                    UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","EmployeeDetail_Error");

                }
            }});
    }

    function RemoveEmployeeFromPayroll(e,EmployeeId,CycleId,PayrollCycleId, transactionDate) {
        var data;
        data = { EmployeeId: EmployeeId, CycleId: CycleId, PayrollCycleId: PayrollCycleId, transactionDate: transactionDate };

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/RemoveEmployeeFromPayroll",
            data: data,
            type: "POST",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {

                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DetailsPopup",data: { id : '622', sourceDataView :  'EmployeesDataView' ,aptaDataViewSelection:aptaDataViewSelection},type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","EmployeeDetail_Error");
                    UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","EmployeeDetail_Error");

                }
            }});
    }

        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").CloseWindow();

    $("#btnAdd__EmployeeJobsDataView").click(function (e) {

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    $("#btnEdit__EmployeeJobsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            EditEmployeeJobFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
        }

    });

    function EditEmployeeJob(EmployeeId, CycleId, JobSequence) {

        var id = EmployeeId + '~' + CycleId + '~' + JobSequence;
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();

        EditEmployeeJobFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    function EditEmployeeJobFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        var data;

        data = { Id: id, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, origin: 1 };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowEmployeeJob")
          .SetIsModal(true)
          .SetContent(options)
          .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
          .SetTitle('Edit Employee Job')
          .SetWidth('1220')
          .SetHeight('90%')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobsDataView", null);

    }

                }
            }
        });
    });

    $("#btnEdit__EmployeeAddressesDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeAddressesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {

            return;

        EditAddressDetails(selectedRowIds);
    });

    $("#btnDelete__EmployeeAddressesDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeAddressesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0) {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?", DeleteEmployeeAddress);
        }
        else {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
        }
    });
    function DeleteEmployeeAddress() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeAddressesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        $("#divEmployeeAddressesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DeleteEmployeeAddress',
            cache: false,
            success: function (result) {

                //refresh grid
                grid.dataSource.read();
                if (result == "") {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Record(s) deleted successfully.", "success", "EmployeeDetail_Error");
                    $("#divEmployeeAddressesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error","EmployeeDetail_Error");
                }

            }
        });
    }

    function RefreshOnDeleteEmployeeJob() {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DeleteEmployeeJob',
                    { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, origin: "1" },
                '', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function DeleteEmployeeJob() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(RefreshOnDeleteEmployeeJob);
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    };

    $("#btnDelete__EmployeeJobsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0)
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?", function () { DeleteEmployeeJob(); });
        else {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
        }
    });

    $("#btnCloseJob__EmployeeJobsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0)
            ShowYesNoDialog("Close Job", "Are you sure you want to close the selected job(s)?", CloseJob);
        else {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
        }
    });

    function RefreshOnCloseJob() {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CloseEmployeeJob', {
            massOpertaionId: massOperationId, selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, origin: "1",
            aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobsDataView")
        }, '', function (result) {
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
        }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function CloseJob() {

        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var showTransactionDatesPopup = 'True';

        var aptaDV = $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        var data = { aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobsDataView"), origin: "1" };
        var encumberWages = false;
        aptaDV.MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DoesIncludeEncumberJob",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                alert(error);
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (showTransactionDatesPopup === "True" &amp;&amp; result.Success == 1) {
                    ShowCloseJobDatePopupEmployeeDetailPopup("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CloseJobEnterDate");
                }
                else {
                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(RefreshOnCloseJob);
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function ShowCloseJobDatePopupEmployeeDetailPopup(contentURL) {

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("EmployeeCloseJobDatePopup")
        .SetContent({ url: contentURL })
        .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
        .SetTitle('Close Job(s)')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeCloseJobDate", null);
    }

    function VacatePosition() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/VacatePositionEmployeeJob',
            success: function (result) {
                grid.dataSource.read();
                if (result == "") {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Job vacated successfully.", "success");
                    $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection()
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    };

    function ShowApproveJobDateEmployeeDetailPopup(contentURL) {
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("EmployeeApproveJobDatePopup")
        .SetContent({ url: contentURL })
        .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
        .SetTitle('Approve Job(s)')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeApproveJobDate", null);
    }

    function RefreshOnApproveJobs(jobID, inProcessRegisterWarning, moveNext, overbudget) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var key = '';
        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/ApproveJob',
                     { jobID: jobID, moveNext: moveNext, massOpertaionId: massOperationId, inProcessRegisterWarning: inProcessRegisterWarning, overbudget: overbudget, origin: "1" },
                key, function (result) {
                    if (result.Success == 1) {
                        RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, false);

                    } else if (result.Success == 3) {
                        if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, true);
                        }
                        else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, true, false);
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Approve Job", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, true); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, true, false); submitForAllNo = e; });

                        }
                    } else if (result.Success == 5) {

                        if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, false, true);
                        }
                        else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, true, true);
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Approve Job", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, false, true); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, true, true); submitForAllNo = e; });

                        }
                    }
                    else if (result.Success == 4) {
                        //4 indicates process end,
                        submitForAllNo = false;
                        submitForAllYes = false;
                        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        ShowMassActionResultsPopup('popupwindowMassActionResults');
                    }
                    else {
                        RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, true);
                    }
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults", false);
    }

    function ApproveJobsWithWarning(inProcessRegisterWarning) {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        // debugger;
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/ApproveJob',
            cache: false,
            data: { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, inProcessRegisterWarning: inProcessRegisterWarning },
            success: function (result) {

                //refresh grid
                grid.dataSource.read();
                if (result == "") {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Job approved successfully.", "success");

                    //removing selection from the attributes.
                    grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected", "");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                }

            }
        });
    }
    var submitForAllNo = false;
    var submitForAllYes = false;
    $('#btnApproveJob__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        submitForAllNo = false;
        submitForAllYes = false;

        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        // check if the config values are present, if yes then show the dialogue.
        var showTransactionDatesPopup = 'True';

        var aptaDV = $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        var data = { aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobsDataView"), origin: "1" };
        aptaDV.MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DoesIncludeEncumberJobWages",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                alert(error);
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (showTransactionDatesPopup === "True" &amp;&amp; result.Success == 1) {
                    ShowApproveJobDateEmployeeDetailPopup("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/ApproveJobEnterDate?fromEmployeeDetailPopup=true");
                }
                else {
                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnApproveJobs(-1, true, false, false); });
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
                }
            }
        });

    });

    function DeleteEmployeeCertificates() {
        //debugger;
        var grid = $("#EmployeeCertificatesDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var sel = grid.tbody.find('tr.k-state-selected');
        var selList = '';
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; sel.length; i++) {
            selList = selList + sel[i].getAttribute('data-aptafund-kendogrid-rowid') + ',';
        }

        $("#divEmployeeCertificatesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DeleteEmployeeCertificates',
            success: function (result) {

                grid.dataSource.read();
                if (result == "") {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Record(s) deleted successfully.", "success", "EmployeeDetail_Error");
                    $("#divEmployeeCertificatesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $("#btnCopyJobToAssignment__EmployeeJobsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        var ids = null;
        var gridData = null;

        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }
        else {
            ids = selectedRowIds.split(',');
            gridData = grid.dataSource.data();
            for (i = 0; i &lt; gridData.length; i++) {
                if (selectedRowIds == -1)
                    ids = [gridData[i].Id];
                if ($.inArray(gridData[i].Id, ids) !== -1) {
                    if (gridData[i].hrViewEmployeeJob__JobStatus === "Closed") {
                        ShowYesNoDialog("Selection", "One or more of the job(s) selected are closed.  Ok to continue?", function ()
                        { CopyJobToAssignment(selectedRowIds); });
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }
            CopyJobToAssignment(selectedRowIds);
        }
    });

    function RefreshOnCopyJobToAssignment(selectedRowIds) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CopyJobToAssignment',
                     { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, selectedRowIds: selectedRowIds, employeeId: '622' },
                '', function (result) {
                    CustomClearGridSelectionAndReload(["#EmployeeAssignmentsDataView", "#EmployeeJobsDataView"],
                "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function CopyJobToAssignment(selectedRowIds) {
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnCopyJobToAssignment(selectedRowIds); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    function DeleteEmployeeAssignments() {

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        $("#divEmployeeAssignmentsDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DeleteEmployeeAssignment',
            success: function (result) {

                grid.dataSource.read();
                if (result.Success == true) {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "EmployeeDetail_Error");
                    $("#divEmployeeAssignmentsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function UpdateImage(imageSource, imageWidth, imageHeight) {

        $("#employeeImage").hide();
        $('#employeeSmallImage').hide();

        $('#employeeSmallImage').attr("src", imageSource);
        $('#employeeSmallImage').attr("alt", "No Picture");

        $("#imageActualWidth").val(imageWidth);
        $("#imageActualHeight").val(imageHeight);
        ResizeImage("employeeSmallImage", 46, 46);

        $('#employeeSmallImage').show();

        $(".EmployeeImageSection").mouseenter(function () {
            $('#employeeSmallImage').css("position", "absolute");
            ResizeImage("employeeSmallImage", 250, 250);
            $('#firstTD').css({ "margin-left": "46px" });
        });

        $(".EmployeeImageSection").mouseleave(function () {
            $('#employeeSmallImage').css("position", "relative");
            ResizeImage("employeeSmallImage", 46, 46);
        });
    }

    function ResizeImage(imageElement, maxiWidth, maxiHeight) {
        var maxWidth = maxiWidth; // Max width for the image
        var maxHeight = maxiHeight;    // Max height for the image
        var ratio = 0;  // Used for aspect ratio

        var width = $("#imageActualWidth").val();
        var height = $("#imageActualHeight").val();

        // Check if the current width is larger than the max
        if (width &gt; maxWidth || width &gt; 46) {
            ratio = maxWidth / width;   // get ratio for scaling image
            $("#" + imageElement).css("width", maxWidth); // Set new width
            $("#" + imageElement).css("height", height * ratio);  // Scale height based on ratio
            height = height * ratio;    // Reset height to match scaled image
            width = width * ratio;    // Reset width to match scaled image
        }

        // Check if current height is larger than max
        if (height &gt; maxHeight || height &gt; 46) {
            ratio = maxHeight / height; // get ratio for scaling image
            $("#" + imageElement).css("height", maxHeight);   // Set new height
            $("#" + imageElement).css("width", width * ratio);    // Scale width based on ratio
            width = width * ratio;    // Reset width to match scaled image
        }
    }
    function OnPageLoad() {
        if ($("#HireDate").val() == '01/01/0001')
            $("#HireDate").val('');
        if ($("#BirthDate").val() == '01/01/0001')
            $("#BirthDate").val('');
        //debugger;
        UpdateImage(smallImageSource,'46', '46');

        var panelBar = $("#panelbar").data("kendoPanelBar");
        var panGeneral = localStorage.getItem("panelSelectedGen");
        var panEmployee = localStorage.getItem("panelSelectedEmp");
        var panCustom = localStorage.getItem("panelSelectedCus");

        if (panEmployee == null &amp;&amp; panCustom == null &amp;&amp; panGeneral == null) {
            panelBar.expand($('#panelbar li:nth-child(1)'))
            panelBar.expand($('#panelbar li:nth-child(2)'))
            panelBar.expand($('#panelbar li:nth-child(3)'))
        }
        else {
            if (panGeneral != null &amp;&amp; panGeneral != "0")
                panelBar.expand($('#panelbar li:nth-child(1)'));
            if (panEmployee != null &amp;&amp; panEmployee != "0")
                panelBar.expand($('#panelbar li:nth-child(2)'));
            if (panCustom != null &amp;&amp; panCustom != "0")
                panelBar.expand($('#panelbar li:nth-child(3)'));
        }
    }

    function EmployeeSave(saveNext, saveAdd, e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "","EmployeeDetail_Error");
        var sendFromEnableDisablEmp = false;
        if(e &amp;&amp; e.target &amp;&amp; (e.target.id == "btnEnableEmployee__Employee" || e.target.id == "btnDisableEmployee__Employee"))
            sendFromEnableDisablEmp = true;

        if ('BCCHS' != $('#Site').val() &amp;&amp; '622' &gt; 0) {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Also Update Payroll Site", "You have changed the employee&amp;#39;s site. Would you like this change to be applied to the employee&amp;#39;s paycheck site in Payroll?", function () { $('#PropagateSiteChangetoPayroll').val(true); SubmitEmployeeForm(saveNext, saveAdd, e, sendFromEnableDisablEmp); }, function () { SubmitEmployeeForm(saveNext, saveAdd, e, sendFromEnableDisablEmp); });
        }
        else{
            SubmitEmployeeForm(saveNext, saveAdd, e, sendFromEnableDisablEmp);
        }
    }

    function SubmitEmployeeForm(saveNext, saveAdd, e, sendFromEnableDisablEmp) {
        var form = $("#FormEmployee");
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: !sendFromEnableDisablEmp,
            url: form.attr('action'),
            data: form.serialize(),
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == true) {
                    if(!sendFromEnableDisablEmp)
                    {
                        MarkEmployeeRecordAsDirty();
                    }
                    if (saveNext) {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "EmployeeDetail_Error");
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'EmployeesDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url : "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DetailsPopup",data: {Id : '',sourceDataView: 'EmployeesDataView',aptaDataViewSelection : aptaDataViewSelection }});
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeesDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        if(grid !== undefined)
                        {
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                        }
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }
                    else if (saveAdd) {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "EmployeeDetail_Error");
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CreatePopup", data:{sourceDataView: 'EmployeesDataView'} });
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeesDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        if(grid !== undefined)
                        {
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                        }
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }
                    else if(622 &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; sendFromEnableDisablEmp){
                        return true;
                    }
                    else if(622 &gt; 0)
                    {
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeesDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        if(grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined){
                            grid.dataSource.read();}
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        var Id = result.EmployeeId;
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DetailsPopup",data:{Id:Id,sourceDataView: result.SourceDataView},type:"POST"});
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeesDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        if(grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined){
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                        }
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "EmployeeDetail_Error");
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","EmployeeDetail_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnEnableEmployee__Employee').click(function (e) {
        ShowYesNoDialog('Enable Employee', "Are you sure that you want to enable this employee?"
           , function() {$.when(EmployeeSave(false,false,e))
                           .then(function() {
                               var data = {employeeId: '622', enabled: true};
                               SetSingleEnableEmployee(data,e)
                           });})
    });

    $('#btnDisableEmployee__Employee').click(function (e) {
        ShowYesNoDialog('Disable Employee', "Are you sure that you want to disable this employee?"
            , function() {$.when(EmployeeSave(false,false,e))
                            .then(function() {
                                var data = { employeeId: '622', enabled: false};
                                SetSingleEnableEmployee(data,e)
                            });})
    });

    function SetSingleEnableEmployee(data,e) {
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/SetSingleEnabledEmployees",
            data: data,
            type: "POST",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    if ($("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView") != undefined) {
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    }
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DetailsPopup",data: { id : '622', sourceDataView :  'EmployeesDataView' ,aptaDataViewSelection:aptaDataViewSelection},type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","EmployeeDetail_Error");
                    UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    if ($("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView") != undefined) {
                        $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();
                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","EmployeeDetail_Error");

                }
            }});
    }

    $("#btnApprove__EmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var grid = $("#EmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!$("#divEmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("AptaDataView")
                .ValidateDataViewGridSelection(false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation."))
            return;

        var arr = selectedRowIds.split(',');
        var empId = arr[0].split('~')[0];

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/VerifyDeductionSetPopup',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if (!result) {
                    ShowOkDialog("Error", "Please select deduction set with new status to perform this operation", null);
                    return;
                }
                else {

                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnProcessApproveDeduction(empId); });
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);

                }
            }
        });

    });

    function RefreshOnProcessApproveDeduction(empId) {

                         { operationResultId: massOperationId, aptaDataViewSelection: $("#divEmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection() },
                    key, function (result) {
                        var grid = $("#EmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                    }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!$("#divEmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.")) return;
        var options = { url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/PreviewNetPay", data: { selectedId: selectedRowIds}, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject('popupPayrollPreviewNetPay')
       .SetContent(options)
       .SetHeight('90%')
       .SetWidth(1170)
       .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
       .SetIsModal(true)
       .SetTitle('Preview Net Pay')

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    function EditEmployeeDeduction(deductionId) {

        var id = deductionId;
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeeDeductionDetailDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        EditEmployeePayrollDeductionScreen(id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }
    $("#btnAdd__EmployeeDeductionDetailDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeductionSetup/CreateDeductionSetUpDetail", data: { EmployeeId: '622', sourceDataView: "EmployeeDeductionDetailDataView"}, type: "POST" };
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject('popupWindowEmployeeDeductionSetup')
      .SetContent(options)
      .SetHeight('90%')
      .SetWidth(1000)
      .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
      .SetIsModal(true)
      .SetTitle('Add Employee Deduction')

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    });

    $("#btnEdit__EmployeeDeductionDetailDataView").click(function (e) {

        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#divEmployeeDeductionDetailDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            EditEmployeePayrollDeductionScreen(0, aptaDataViewSelection)
        }
    });

    function EditEmployeePayrollDeductionScreen(id,aptaDataViewSelection)
    {
        var options = { url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeductionSetup/Detail", data: { id: id, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, sourceDataView: "EmployeeDeductionDetailDataView" }, type: "POST" };
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject('popupWindowEmployeeDeductionSetup')
    .SetContent(options)
    .SetHeight('90%')
    .SetWidth(1050)
    .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
    .SetIsModal(true)
    .SetTitle('Edit Employee Deduction')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    }

    function FixIE10Content() {

        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");

            }
        }
